[{\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"The biggest problem automated vehicles solve is that human beings are not well-suited to traveling at high speeds.  As speed increases, our time and distance perception degrades.  We do not have a sufficient range of lateral vision and no rear vision.  We are limited in our ability to focus and process data and we tend to focus on one thing at a time (which leads to distraction from the task of driving).  In short, we make mistakes behind the wheel and these mistakes (including outright negligence like driving under the influence) are the primary cause in more than 90% of accidents.\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"So the biggest benefit is the capacity to prevent human errors that lead to accidents, injuries, and deaths.\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"Using a strict definition of driverless car as meaning a car the drives without any human supervision or even a human on board, the largest benefit involves higher efficiency in vehicle use.  Right now, when I am not using my car, it still has to stay where I can get to it.  Driverless vehicles turn this around.  Now the car has to be where it can get to me when I need it.  So during the downtime when I am not using the car, the car can be doing other things.\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"And from a humanitarian standpoint, driverless cars will provide mobility to people who otherwise would have few or no ways of getting around.
